***подтолкнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подтолкнуть.html>подтолкну́ть</a> (7386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкнуть.html>толкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтолкнуть.html>подтолкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podtolknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подталкивать.html>подта́лкивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to nudge, to push slightly</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to encourage, to urge on</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толк</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:подталкивать.html>подта́лкивать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>под-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-толк-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***подтягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a> (12743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">подтяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podtjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podtjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to pull up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to haul up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>бе́регу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podtjágivatʹ</b> brevnó k béregu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull the log to the shore</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ше</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podtjágivatʹ</b> brevnó k krýše</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to haul the log onto the roof</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring up, to move closer up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of troops, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to tighten</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tuck in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam nádo <b>podtjanútʹ</b> anglíjskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you must pull up your English (to a better standard)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дисциплина.html>дисципли́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podtjágivatʹ</b> disciplínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tighten up discipline</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to help catch up with the rest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to join in singing, to join in a song, to sing along, to harmonize</li></ol>

***подтягиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подтягиваться.html>подтя́гиваться</a> (17013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podtjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягиваться.html>подтя́гиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podtjágivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуться.html>подтяну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten one's belt</li>
<li>to pull oneself up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve one's standard, to catch up with the rest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуться.html>подтяну́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йскому</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam nado podtjanútʹsja po anglíjskomu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you must pull up your English (to a better standard)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to brace oneself up, to pull oneself together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move up, to move in</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podtjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podtjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягивать.html>подтя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to pull up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to haul up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>бе́регу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podtjanútʹ</b> brevnó k béregu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull the log to the shore</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бревно.html>бревно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ше</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podtjanútʹ</b> brevnó k krýše</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to haul the log onto the roof</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to bring up, to move closer up <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of troops, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to tighten</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tuck in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pull up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam nádo <b>podtjanútʹ</b> anglíjskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you must pull up your English (to a better standard)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дисциплина.html>дисципли́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podtjanútʹ</b> disciplínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tighten up discipline</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to help catch up with the rest</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to join in singing, to join in a song, to sing along, to harmonize</li></ol>

***подтянуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуться.html>подтяну́ться</a> (11073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podtjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуться.html>подтяну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podtjanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтягиваться.html>подтя́гиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten one's belt</li>
<li>to pull oneself up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve one's standard, to catch up with the rest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуться.html>подтяну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йскому</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vam nado <b>podtjanútʹsja</b> po anglíjskomu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you must pull up your English (to a better standard)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to brace oneself up, to pull oneself together</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move up, to move in</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подтянуть.html>подтяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podtjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

Зализняка — 3c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:подтягиваться.html>подтя́гиваться</a>.

<li>to go quickly, to scamper</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start blowing</li></ol>

***подушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шка</a> (2206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">подушька</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podušĭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*podušьka</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>по́душка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póduška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">роduškа</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">роduškа</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">poduszka</i>. Derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*poduxa</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">по́духа</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póduxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/History_of_the_Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:History of the Czech language">Old Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-ocs">poducha</i>); also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duxъna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feather-bedspread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately derivable from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duxъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breath, spirit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, through the sense development "breath" → "inflated" → "pillow".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pillow, cushion</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подушечка.html>поду́шечка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podúšečka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***подхват.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подхват.html>подхва́т</a> (25156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхватить.html>подхвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхват.html>подхва́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podxvát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхват.html>подхва́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхват.html>подхва́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхват.html>подхва́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> picking up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> catching</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> joining in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подхват.html>подхва́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>podxváte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ready to carry out an assignment</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>log supported lengthwise in an adit in a mine</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхватить.html>подхвати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podxvatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхватывать.html>подхва́тывать</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подхватывать.html>подхва́тывать</a> (9562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхватить.html>подхвати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podxvatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхватывать.html>подхва́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podxvátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подхватить.html>подхвати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch (up), to pick up, to grasp, to snatch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch, to pick up (a disease)</li>
<li>to pick up (an expression, a song)</li>
<li>to join in, to take up, to catch up</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***подходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подходить.html>подходи́ть</a> (857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подходить.html>подходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подойти.html>подойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fit (of an object, to match another object)</li>
<li>to come up (to), to approach, to go up (to)</li>
<li>to approach</li>
<li>to do (for); to suit</li>
<li>to arrive, to come</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цепи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-cepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
